### BREAKING CHANGE

- accordion trigger is now a directive & accordion icon is replaced with hlm-icon + directive
- Angular 20 is no longer supported. spartan/ui now
  supports Angular 21 and 22.

- ci: lower unit test parallelism to fit the runner memory

The docs app's vitest + Analog suite peaks at a few GB; running it
alongside two other test projects under --parallel=3 exhausted the
GitHub runner memory and the worker was OOM-killed with no output.
Run at most two test projects concurrently.

- fix(trpc): drop invalid environment providers from the test env module

The Nx 22 migration wrapped provideZoneChangeDetection() in an @NgModule,
but EnvironmentProviders are not valid in @NgModule providers and Angular
21 throws NG0207 at runtime. Restore the plain initTestEnvironment setup
(matching the docs app); the explicit zone provider is unnecessary.

- ci: run the docs app test suite in isolation

Bundling the docs app's vitest + Analog suite into the parallel test run
made it fail in CI while it passes on its own, and the interleaved output
hid the cause. Run the other projects in parallel, then the docs app as a
separate step.

- fix(nx): point test cache inputs at the real jest preset file

The test targets' cache inputs referenced jest.preset.js, but the
workspace preset is jest.preset.cjs, so the input never matched and a
preset change would not invalidate the cache. Fix both the
@nx/vitest:test target (added by the Nx 22 migration) and the existing
@nx/jest:jest target.

- ci: log exit code and retry the docs app test suite once

The docs app's vitest + Analog suite intermittently crashes in CI right
after loading Angular's testing modules, with no error output. Log the
exit code to classify the crash (128+signal indicates a native crash)
and retry once so a flaky crash does not fail the run while the root
cause is investigated.

- ci: clarify docs app test retry after pinpointing the flaky crash

The crash is in app.spec.ts: booting the full app shell (Header/Footer
and their deep import graph) intermittently crashes the vitest worker
during the Analog transform in CI (exit 1, no output, not reproducible
locally). It happens before any test runs, so a vitest per-test retry
cannot help; re-running the suite once does.

- chore(repo): hold analog at 2.1.3 and drop unit-test ci workarounds

Analog 2.6.0 intermittently crashed the docs app's vitest worker in CI
(a flaky transform of the app shell), so keep analog at the nx-migration's
tested 2.1.3, revert the marked bumps that 2.6.0 required, and restore the
ai-chat-link directive selector. Also restore the original unit test ci
step, dropping the parallel, isolation and retry workarounds added while
chasing that crash.

- remove the closeDelay input and configuration option. Remove explicit delay
  values; closed-state exit animations are now detected automatically.
- Renamed useAutoColor to autoColor, userCls to userClass
- Tailwind CSS v3 is no longer supported. The
  @spartan-ng/brain/hlm-tailwind-preset (JS) package export has been removed; use
  the @spartan-ng/brain/hlm-tailwind-preset.css preset with Tailwind CSS v4. The
  tailwindcss peer dependency now requires >=4.0.0.
- the unused accordion/collapsible measurement config has been
  removed: `provideBrnAccordionConfig`, `injectBrnAccordionConfig`,
  `provideBrnCollapsibleConfig`, `injectBrnCollapsibleConfig`, their config types,
  and the `measureDimensions` helper. The `measurementDisplay` option no longer
  exists; content height is now measured automatically.
